## ğŸ“¦ Installation & Usage

1. Clone the repository  
   ```bash
   git clone https://github.com/Abdallahosama55/GenieLamp.git
   cd GenieLamp
   ```
2. Install dependencies  
   ```bash
   npm install
   ```
3. Run the project  
   ```bash
   npm run dev
   ```
